<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%; text-indent:-2%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Items 1 through 7 are not included because they are not applicable. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%; text-indent:-2%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Item 8.01. <U>Other Events</U>. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%; text-indent:-2%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><U>Filing of Computational Materials</U> </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In connection with the offering of the GMACM Mortgage Pass-Through Certificates, Series
2004-J6 (the &#147;<U>Certificates</U>&#148;), each of Credit Suisse First Boston LLC and Countrywide Securities Corporation (the &#147;<U>Underwriters</U>&#148;) has prepared certain materials (the &#147;<U>Computational Materials</U>&#148;) for
distribution to potential investors. Although Residential Asset Mortgage Products, Inc. (the &#147;<U>Company</U>&#148;) provided the Underwriters with certain information regarding the characteristics of the mortgage loans (the &#147;<U>Mortgage
Loans</U>&#148;) in the related portfolio, the Company did not participate in the preparation of the Computational Materials. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For purposes of this Form 8-K, &#147;<U>Computational Materials</U>&#148; shall mean computer generated tables and/or charts displaying, with respect to the Certificates,
any of the following: yield; average life; duration, expected maturity; interest rate sensitivity; cash flow characteristics; background information regarding the Mortgage Loans; the proposed structure; decrement tables; or similar information
(tabular or otherwise) of a statistical, mathematical, tabular or computational nature. The Computational Materials listed as <U>Exhibit 99.</U>1 were filed on Form SE dated December 29, 2004. These Computational Materials consist of the pages that
appear after the Form SE cover sheet. The Computational Materials listed as <U>Exhibit 99.2</U> were filed on Form SE dated December 30, 2004. These Computational Materials consist of the pages that appear after the Form SE cover sheet. The
Computational Materials listed as <U>Exhibit 99.3</U> are filed electronically. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%; text-indent:-2%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Item 9.01. <U>Financial Statements and Exhibits</U> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT
